宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">达日（藏）都是四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，二人皆因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名分别重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">臧金达：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西咸阳市法轮功学员。咸阳市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张鹏、王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏因为向淳化县民众发放真相资料，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月先后在各自的住所被淳化县公安局警察抓捕抄家。张鹏、王钰超（<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁左右）<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底在咸阳市住处被警察绑架，电脑、打印机等设备被抢走。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位法轮功学员被关押在咸阳淳化县看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均已被判刑，其中张鹏判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，王钰超、臧金达、马海鹏约为<span lang="EN-US">5</span>至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年不等，刑期不详。。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/30/2021-8-30.html#zip3</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">臧中美：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生。吉林省白城法轮功学员。臧中美原是吉林省梨树农场一名小学女教师，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年末因去北京上访被劳教一年半，释放回家后，丈夫和幼小的孩子因经受不住长期的警察上门骚扰被迫离婚。因她不放弃信仰，也被学校开除，流离失所到白城市打工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，臧中美骑电瓶车宣讲法轮功被白城市洮北区国保大队抓捕，并在其住处抄走大法书籍、电脑、真相资料、现金等物品。后被批捕。曾正在看守所绝食反迫害。臧中美<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现关押在长春女子监狱十三大队。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">泽让旦真（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州人，又叫“洛桑丹增”，阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因帮助同寺僧人彭措（又叫平措，已于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日自焚死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁）以自焚方式（指一种藏人抗议暴政、伸张正义的方式，即藏人自焚者把自己整个奉献出来，以清晰的理智、自愿的心态和惨烈的方式向暴政表达最强烈抗议的无奈选择，以期使公众舆论对极权和高压统治者予以最强烈的谴责或改变对手的情感），纪念中共当局镇压拉萨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件三周年，并在阿坝县城洽唐中街实施自焚行动；由于当地僧人和藏人为此举行了大规模情愿示威活动，随与中共军警发生冲突；其随后即被拉萨市警方抓捕、刑拘，并被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康县警方以涉嫌“购买汽油策划，鼓动、帮助自焚罪”执行逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案在四川省马尔康县法院开庭受审，最终被该法院更换罪名，以“故意杀人罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曾春智：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年出生，湖北省孝感市人，孝感市下属应城市居民，应城市海山小区业主，维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年冠状病毒感染疫情蔓延以来，湖北省应城市共有业主<span lang="EN-US">3689</span>户、<span lang="EN-US">8012</span>人，曾先后确诊<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人，隔离密切接触者<span lang="EN-US">41</span>人；当地政府虽为此封闭管控，但因物业管理不规范，导致生活物资配送价格过高，进而引发居民强烈不满；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，因其与亲友、业主近百人在所居海山小区聚集，并高喊“海山物业下课，解散业委会”等口号，以表达对物业公司利用疫情强取豪夺之抗议，遂遭当地方当局的强烈打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被应城市警方以调查取证带头抗议事件为由带走，并被行政拘留数日；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，又被转为刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被应城市检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕；后遭起诉，判刑。后获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。目前被羁押于孝感市应城市看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/3.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/3.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，江西九江法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年出生，九江德安县某学校教师，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被逮捕，于同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日江西省九江市永修县法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年罚金一万，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日二审由九江中级法院，维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曾繁杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省梅州市梅县区法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">. 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时左右，曾繁杰在租住处遭梅州市公安局梅江分局金山派出所警察等抓捕，后被劫持到梅县区（扶大）看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日遭庭审，仅<span lang="EN-US">20</span>分钟便草草收场。后悉，曾繁杰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年并勒索<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万元罚金。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曾凡锦：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，山东省菏泽市人，山东省郓城县育才路东段<span lang="EN-US">123</span>号公民，山东省郓城县公安局原经侦大队指导员，实名举报人，蒙冤警察。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2009</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，曾因和<span lang="EN-US">35</span>名警察联名向上级有关部门实名举报时任山东省郓城县县委书记刘国生严重贪污腐败，滥用职权操控黑白两道，强拆强占农民土地及打死打伤、肆意拘留农民等问题，并将此事发于网上，随遭被举报贪官刘国生等人严厉打压与疯狂报复；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其被不明身份数十人突然夜闯家中非法抄家和绑架，并送菏泽市东郊一处郓城县检察院私设审讯点关押，三天后被莫名刑拘；关押期间，该检察院副院长亲自带队，为让其在已捏造好的莫须有罪名签字认罪，采取连续<span lang="EN-US">50</span>天“车轮战”式审讯、长时间坐老虎凳和不给吃喝等多种酷刑对其折磨，甚至不惜另抓<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名与其关系不错的同事警察，以威逼利诱，酷刑折磨、逼疯逼残等方式强逼他们指控和捏造其犯罪事实；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其被转正式逮捕，后被菏泽市郓城县法院被以“贪污罪”枉法冤判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；后因其不服上诉，经菏泽市中级法院二审裁决，减为<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日获释后，其继续实名举报，并就刘国生、郑建生等官员的贪腐问题和其在狱中曾遭长期刑讯逼供，导致生命几经濒危等事实依法提起申诉；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，刘国生因贪腐落马锒铛入狱，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日终被山东省泰安市中级法院以“受贿罪”从轻判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年；然而其早先为举报贪官而提起的申诉控告，却因山东当局官官相护，始终毫无结果；为求公道正义，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其遂网上发布《抬棺决斗宣言》，并于同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月抬棺向山东司法机关发起生死决斗和法理辩论；此举一出，立时引来社会热议，但也旋即引起山东当局的极度不悦与强力打击；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，再度被当地警方抓捕，后被移交至山东省巨野县看守所刑拘；一个月后，被巨野县检察院以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，被山东省菏泽市巨野县法院以同罪名一审枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年；二审维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。目前疑在山东省菏泽监狱（山东省菏泽市定陶路<span lang="EN-US">61</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">274030</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾尉英：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月生，女，家住鹤山市鹤城镇新联管区。曾尉英因修炼法轮功、并向大众宣传法轮功是教人向善，随被人恶意举报。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾尉英被当地警方带走关押，其家被查抄。之后不久，其案很被构陷到检察院和江门市蓬江区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾尉英广东省江门市蓬江区法院被以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。现在广东省女子监狱二监区服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/2/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E7%9C%81%E9%B9%A4%E5%B1%B1%E5%B8%82%E6%9B%BE%E5%B0%89%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-430343.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/2/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E7%9C%81%E9%B9%A4%E5%B1%B1%E5%B8%82%E6%9B%BE%E5%B0%89%E8%8B%B1%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-430343.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾小莉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东蕉岭县法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚饭后，曾小莉在家中被抓捕、抄家，被抢走大法书籍多本，还有法轮大法师父法像和<span lang="EN-US">1</span>些真相资料及<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘等私人物品。她被关押在梅州市蕉岭县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾小莉被逮捕，后被梅县区法院判处<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年刑期，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">50000</span>元。曾小莉不服提起上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，梅州市中级法院却枉法裁定维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/5/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E8%95%89%E5%B2%AD%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9B%BE%E5%B0%8F%E8%8E%89%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-430441.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/5/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E8%95%89%E5%B2%AD%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9B%BE%E5%B0%8F%E8%8E%89%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-430441.html</span></a></span><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾又梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省聊城市东昌府区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被抓捕抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月庭审。曾又梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾志远：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省邵东市（原邵东县）水东江镇牛山村法轮功学员。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，曾志远多次被中共抓捕，三次被劳教，两次被判刑，在看守所、劳教所、监狱共被关押迫害十多年。曾志远<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被邵东市国保大队警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被邵东市法院判刑五年，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬被关押到娄底监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">扎西达杰（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，炉霍寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。因中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，引发多地藏民强烈不满，四川省甘孜州炉霍县藏民随于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日（即当年中国农历新年初一）举行大规模和平示威活动；该活动随即遭到中共警方严厉的武力镇压和任意抓捕，致使多人被打死打伤及上百人被抓；至<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，已有<span lang="EN-US">36</span>人被中共当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月直至无期徒刑不等的刑期，另有数人被捕后完全失踪；扎西达杰亦因积极参与和平示威游行，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被警方以“参与和带头示威活动”为由从当地炉霍寺抓走刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以“炉火示威活动的主要带头人”判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。此前被羁押于四川省甘孜藏族自治州康定县监狱；目前在何监狱服刑，情况不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">扎西顿珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县唐克镇人。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因独自在四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县城，身披佛教旗帜、手举大幅达赖喇嘛画像，以小跑方式在主要大道上开展抗议中共暴政的示威活动，随被当地警方在极短时间内控制、拘捕；据悉，此前其所在村镇藏民多年来一直因土地遭政府强占、暴力逼迁且得不到任何安置，而多次展开过和平请愿活动（含派代表进省城上访、集体静坐、呈交联署信、集会讨公道等），要求政府当局核实土地征用过程是否非法，并予以公正处理，但却无果而终；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，其被阿坝藏族羌族自治州地方当局正式逮捕，并被判处有期徒刑，罪名、刑期不详，服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">扎西杰（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县人。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因拍录阿坝藏族羌族自治州藏人扎西顿珠身披佛教旗帜、手举大幅达赖喇嘛画像，在若尔盖县城大街上进行抗议中共暴政的抗议过程，并传于网上，随被当地警方于<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日左右抓捕、刑拘，具体罪由不详；据悉，此前其所在乡镇藏民长期因土地问题而被政府强占、暴力逼迁，得不到安置等所困扰，村民多次展开和平请愿活动而无果；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，其与扎西顿珠一起被阿坝藏族羌族自治州地方当局正式逮捕，并被判处有期徒刑，罪名、刑期不详，服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">扎西曲英（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，四川省甘孜州道孚县葛卡乡约呷村人，道孚县尼措寺（全名“尼措图桑达杰林寺”，汉文称“灵雀寺”）僧人，印度西藏甘丹寺强孜经学院最高等级“格西拉然巴”经学博士班一年级学生，藏族政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年前往印度，同年进入印度南部西藏甘丹寺强孜经学院学习。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月下旬持中国驻新德里大使馆发放的旅行证返家探亲过程中，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日突然被中共当局毫无理由地强行拘捕，至此失联。后获悉其被当局指控，因在印度期间曾将道孚县境内发生自焚事件的消息披露给媒体，随被视为泄密。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底，经一位藏族政治犯从监狱获释后向其家人传信，家人方才获知，他和扎西曲英在同一个监狱服刑，扎西曲英被监禁在甘孜州首府康定县新都桥镇的四川省甘孜监狱。后经证实，他于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被四川省甘孜州法院以不知名罪名（疑似“泄露国家机密罪等”）重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">翟永池：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">辽宁省绥中县人，法轮功学员。因信仰、宣传法轮功遭多次打压逼迫。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被辽宁省绥中县警方以涉邪教罪刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被转正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日其案在辽宁省绥中县法院开庭受审，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”一审判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。其不服，已上诉到葫芦岛市中级法院，律师递交了开庭申请，即将面临二审。目前被羁押于绥中县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">詹传云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽省长丰县女访民。其家房屋被拆迁、土地被征收，因未获合理补偿而上访。詹传云女士是于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被警方从家中抓捕后刑拘羁押于合肥女子看守所的，被羁押<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天才开庭审理。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，詹传云被敲诈勒索（政府）罪案件在长丰县人民法院第二法庭开庭审理，詹传云女士的律师作了无罪辩护，合肥市<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多位访民到庭旁听案件审理。据悉，案件审理时，公诉人提出的证据被律师驳回，女访民岂能敲诈政府？尤其是敲诈国家暴力机器公安部门，案件审理将结束时，迫于证据难以支持敲诈勒索罪的法官问被告人詹传云，撤掉敲诈勒索罪变更为寻衅滋事罪行不行？被告人詹传云女士非常坚定的回答，她没有罪。最后陈述时，詹传云女士称自己为自己家房屋被拆迁和土地征收上访维权，她没有罪。最终，法院仍判处詹传云<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">帖林峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省南阳市<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁的法轮功学员，其妻子何喜梅退休前曾在南阳市沼气（现郑燃南阳燃气）公司任营业所长，一九九七年开始修炼法轮大法，在工作中，何喜梅兢兢业业干好本职工作，多次被单位、建委、省建设厅评为：“先进科室”、“建委十佳职工”、“省建设厅职业道德先进个人”等荣誉。她丈夫帖林峰也修炼法轮大法。一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，何喜梅和帖林峰曾多次遭中共迫害。何喜梅和丈夫帖林峰夫妻两人<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日都被南阳市公安局抓捕，关押在南阳市看守所。后获悉，何喜梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金三万元；帖林峰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金一万元。何喜梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。帖林峰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52187221"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">展中香：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52187221;"></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，山东平度市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日与好友周玉香和周君一起到平度仁兆赶集，被仁兆派出所警察抓捕。后，展中香和周玉香分别被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，周君被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张宝成：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1959</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日出生，北京市人，自由职业者，资深民主人士，新公民运动参与者，北京西单广场举牌十公民之一。因张宝成于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年起开始积极参与推动中国的民主活动，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年春被北京市警方关押；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年年底，又因声援刘远东而被警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，再次因积极参与“官员财产公示”活动，于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，张宝成与袁冬等人同时被北京市公安局公共交通安全保卫分局以涉嫌“非法集会罪”刑事拘留，并被关押于北京市海淀区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被北京市警方正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被北京市海淀区法院以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”开庭审理；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被北京市海淀区法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，刑满释放；据悉，其在狱中曾遭受虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月底，六四<span lang="EN-US">30</span>周年临近，中共当局的维稳镇压措施愈来愈严厉，北京民主维权人士张宝成也被抓捕、抄家。据张宝成妻子刘珏帆介绍：“北京时间<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日零时许，女儿接到张宝成用家里座机打出的电话，他又被抓了，正在抄家，警察说是涉枪。 张宝成不可能涉枪，我怀疑张宝成被抓与他推特转发有关即将来临的敏感日帖子有关。”<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>：<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分张宝成“寻衅滋事、宣扬恐怖主义、极端主义”案在北京市第二中级法院<span lang="EN-US">A</span>座第<span lang="EN-US">12</span>法庭开庭 。未当庭宣判。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">后张宝成案于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日上午在北京二中院宣判，张宝成获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，其中被以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被以宣扬恐怖主义、极端主义罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，合并执行<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日张宝成案二审北京高院今天上午<span lang="EN-US">9:30</span>宣判：驳回上诉，维持原判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_97.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_97.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">张宝玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，辽宁瓦房店市复州城镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，张宝玲、姜淑波与慈美云三名老年女法轮功学员，去讲三台乡讲清法轮功被迫害真相，被辽宁省大连市三台乡派出所抓捕、关押、抄家。随后送瓦房店看守所隔离关押半个月后，羁押在大连姚家看守所。后被批捕。张宝玲、姜淑波、慈美云于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月二<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日开庭。后张宝玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，姜淑波被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张朝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省潍坊市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日下午，张朝被当地警方抓捕到看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，张朝被潍坊市奎文区检察院批捕，所谓罪名是：以危险方法危害公共安全罪和妨害公务罪。据说，因此次事件国保谷志勇和奎文公安局长曹俊勇还被予以立功行为。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分，山东省潍坊市法轮功学员张朝，在潍坊市奎文区法院，第三次被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张乘豪</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：山西省太原市人，基督徒，山西省太原市晋源区古县城<span lang="EN-US">"</span>郇城归正教会<span lang="EN-US">"</span>同工，中国在押良心犯。因笃信耶稣基督而成为基督徒，并在太原市晋源区古县城郇城归正教会做同工（即为教会一起努力侍奉、祷告、义务服务的人），又因所在教会是家庭教会，属于中共山西当局收编利诱或打击拆毁的对象，故其在教会的活动深受当局监控和骚扰<span lang="EN-US">;2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底，因曾与郇城教会传道人安彦魁及教会在山西省临汾市的同工 张立功、张耀文、 王润云、王世强、宋守山等人一同前往马来西亚首都吉隆坡，参加著名基督教华人布道家和神学家唐崇荣牧师组织的<span lang="EN-US">"2020</span>福音与文化大会<span lang="EN-US">"</span>，尽管当时其持个人护照及签证出入海关一切正常，且无任何违法行为，但返回一年半之后，却因此引起中共山西当局的高度警觉与不满<span lang="EN-US">;2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，突然被山西省汾阳市警方带走传唤，家遭查抄，其夫妇二人的手机、计算机等私人对象被搜走，后其被以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US"> "</span>偷越国（边）境罪<span lang="EN-US">"</span>刑拘，并与郇城教会传道人安彦魁同属一案<span lang="EN-US">;2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，又被汾阳市检察院以涉嫌同罪名予以批捕<span lang="EN-US">;</span>据悉，其妻郭娟随后亦被传唤，后曾在与所聘代理律师去看守所为其递送衣物时，律师申请与其会见，遭警方拒绝，并被告知其案因涉及国家安全与机密，办案单位已给看守所下发不准会见通知书。目前被羁押于汾阳市孝义市看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/568.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/568.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张春蕾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西忻州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，张春蕾因要求各级政府公开关于迫害法轮功的政策而被非法抓捕。后被批捕，起诉。罪名是利用邪教破坏法律实施罪。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午忻州市忻府区法院开庭审理张春蕾利用邪教破坏法律实施案，文东海律师作为辩护律师参与开庭审理，该案检察院不让辩护律师阅卷，不接收辩护律师手续，不听取辩护律师意见。到了法院仍然不允许阅卷，不公开审理，没有庭审录音录像，在庭上只有法官检察官可以看卷，辩护律师和被告人均不让看卷，辩护律师拒绝就检察官口头念的证据目录发表质证意见，申请回避驳回，要求复议法官认为没有复议权利。后遭判刑，刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张春雷</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：贵阳仁爱归正教会长老。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，贵阳仁爱归正教会信众和几位外地来的基督徒在教会租的温州大酒店商住楼<span lang="EN-US">1702</span>房祷告，遭警方冲击，三位本地基督徒陈建国、李金芝和李林，以及从贵阳周边过来参加学习的基督徒共十人被带到延安中路派出所。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点左右，仁爱归正教会的张春雷长老赶到派出所交涉。在与派出所工作人员交涉过程中，张春雷长老被警察粗暴地推到在地，并遭扣押。后张春雷长老先是被口头通知行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">11</span>天，但到期后未被释放。家属被口头告知张春雷长老已被刑事拘留但没有收到任何法律手续，主动询问办案单位和派出所，告知法律手续已寄出。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">中午，张春雷的妻子杨爱清师母去往派出所，拿到了贵阳市公安局云岩分局针对张春雷长老的逮捕通知书。据通知书所述，经贵阳市云岩区检察院批准，张春雷长老于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日<span lang="EN-US">15</span>时被以涉嫌诈骗罪的名义执行逮捕，羁押在云岩分局看守所。后转入贵阳市第二看守所。继<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日到<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日律师连续四天会见因遭遇到提审未见到以后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，律师会见张春雷长老再次受阻。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午九点，律师持会见手续到贵阳市第二看守所要求会见此前因被控“诈骗罪”而被羁押张春雷长老。接待民警称不能会见，理由是贵阳市国安局<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日向看守所发函，告知张春雷因涉嫌危害国家安全，在侦查期间未得到办案单位允许的情况下，禁止律师会见。律师要求对该文件复印或者拍照，被看守所民警拒绝。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">张翠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">辽宁大连市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年代生人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被抓捕并于当日晚上被批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被甘井子区法院视频开庭，后被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金两万元。张翠不服判决向大连市中级法院上诉，中院于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日对张翠视频开庭，维持原判。张翠的退休金于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被停发。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/17/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436935.html#22116224158-6"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/17/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436935.html#22116224158-6</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">张翠娟<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">广州市花都区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年出生，家住广州市花都区商业大道；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被广州市公安局花都区分局警察抓捕，关押到花都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被荔湾区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/27/2022-1-27.html#zip6"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/27/2022-1-27.html#zip6</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张德武：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">民营企业家、湖北襄大集团董事长。襄大集团是湖北省知名民营企业，上世纪<span lang="EN-US">90</span>年代，张德武从送鸡苗起步，白手起家创业，目前集团主营业务为农业畜牧养殖，并涉及化工以及房地产开发等，拥有襄大农牧、新鄂西化工、襄大建筑、襄大物流等生产经营板块，资产<span lang="EN-US">76</span>亿元人民币，员工<span lang="EN-US">7,100</span>余人。襄大集团曾在当地政府动员下，斥资七亿、承债式收购一个濒临破产的国企改制化工厂。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，因为张德武和债权人协商未果，债权人将化工厂告上法庭，襄阳中级法院便冻结了企业的基本账户。化工厂职工养老金停发、社保停缴，职工医疗费用无法报销。随后，将近八百名鄂西化工厂职工集体有序来到襄阳中院门口，聚集上访。此事被指为涉嫌“聚众冲击国家机关”，成为<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年张德武涉黑案的导火索。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，张德武及公司多名负责人被以涉嫌“聚众冲击国家机关罪”带走，继而被以涉黑移送审查起诉。一年后，张德武在<span lang="EN-US">17</span>年前，即<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年已审结无罪的一桩旧案，又被检察院重新提起抗诉。张德武被捕后，当地养殖户、村民、供应商纷纷站出来为其请愿，联名上书。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，湖北襄大集团董事长张德武被湖北省竹溪县法院一审认定犯寻衅滋事罪、非法拘禁罪、串通投标罪、高利转贷罪、聚众冲击国家机关罪，被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">6013</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/13.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/13.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张迪</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张凤兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，女、哈尔滨市宾县宾州镇第二小学退休教师，<span lang="EN-US">998</span>年十<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共邪党开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，张凤兰被中共邪党抓捕、关押，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，张凤兰在讲述法轮功真相时，遭不明真相的人构陷，被哈尔滨市宾县公安局警察抓捕、抄家。当天，张凤兰被哈尔滨市宾县公安局国保警察关押到哈尔滨市第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，她被哈尔滨市依兰县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">张改从：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河北省深泽县法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被抓捕，一直被关押在第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月份，被开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉，张改从被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/14/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436824.html#2211322315-2"><b minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张桂淑：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，北京市顺义区杨镇下坡村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被顺义区杨镇派出所抓捕，经<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月的等待，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，法院以手机信息提示在顺义开庭审理，以疫情为由，拒绝家属旁听。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月份，家属在看守所咨询后，得知张桂淑被判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，期间未接到过任何部门以任何方式通知家属判决情况。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434070.html#211125222822-2"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/26/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AD%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434070.html#211125222822-2</span></a></span><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张国兵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东河源维权人士。张国兵有两个孩子的，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日以学生家长身份依法申请公布学校食品安全监督信息。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>时被东源县公安带走，约三小时后被广东河源市公安局人员抄家。搜走手机、身份证、护照、银行卡等物（张没有电脑）。家属两次都问公安人员，是什么事抓人？均回答，不知道，查清楚再说。后获悉<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪名被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日广东省河源县法院以寻衅滋事罪判处张国兵有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，没收作案工具苹果手机<span lang="EN-US">1</span>部，<span lang="EN-US">NOKIA</span>牌手机<span lang="EN-US">1</span>部。 判决依据的所谓犯罪事实是，张国兵多次翻墙使用推待和注册使用微信发表和转发一些涉嫌不实和诋毁国家党政领导人、抨击国家制度的负面言论信息，造成严重的不良社会影响。张国兵刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张海涛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年出生，河南省南阳市镇平县籍人，原<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代国企下岗工人，新疆区域电信产品销售者、自由职业者，民主人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被新疆维吾尔族自治区乌鲁木齐市中亚南路派出所警方以涉嫌“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”抄家、刑事拘留、逮捕；之后被以“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕，羁押于新疆乌鲁木齐市看守所。据悉，其家中银行卡全部被警方冻结，妻子即将生育，生活面临极大困境。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日再次被变更罪名以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”继续超期关押，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被乌鲁木齐中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家罪”、“为境外刺探、非法提供情报罪”重判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处没收个人财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">12</span>万；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日经新疆乌鲁木齐高级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判。目前在新疆维吾尔族自治区沙雅监狱九监区服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张慧岩：原</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省通化市柳河县白酒厂技术员，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，流离失所十年的法轮功学员张慧岩被抓捕。当年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，家属接到公主岭监狱电话才得知，张慧岩被柳河县判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被送进吉林省公主岭市监狱，目前已两个多月，家人不允许见面。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张健：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省长春市法轮功学员。张健于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被长春市二道公安分局东盛路派出所抓捕，在苇子沟拘留所被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日后送至长春市第三看守所，转为刑事拘留，后被朝阳区检察院起诉。听说张健现在被非法关押在宋家新建的一个羁押场所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，张健家属得到有关部门通知，张健被视频开庭，非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/27/2021-12-27.html#211226224726-2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张荆州：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，原湖北省荆州市金隆集团公司员工，法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功，张荆州已被处罚<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次：<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚上，荆州市公安局指挥，沙市开发区公安局和燎原派出所十几个警察在出租屋，抓捕了张荆州与邵廉，并抄家，抢走打印纸<span lang="EN-US">2</span>十多箱，打印机约<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>台，电脑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台，还有裁纸刀等物品。张荆州、邵廉被关押在荆州西门看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，张荆州被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；邵廉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张敬元：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林农安县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员。此次抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的。此次被抓捕的法轮功学员有</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张秀芝、高晓歧、蔡玉英、吴冬梅、于姣茹、单为和、赵秀兰、孙秀英、张敬元、孙凤仙、冯立齐、吕相富、董秀辉等<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">22</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。他们被抓捕、构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：张敬元被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，张敬元被送到公主岭监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html"><span
