lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周妍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">46</span>岁，黑龙江哈尔滨法轮功学员。哈尔滨市哈尔滨市依兰县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午对依兰县、佳木斯市桦川县两地法轮功学员实施绑架，到<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日共有<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人被绑架，其中十四名法轮功学员宋玉芝、施凤香、施凤兰、王云杰、周妍、邓术梅、宋孔华、武桂琴、卜宝玲、夏桂华、唐立飞、姚怀英、康艳玲、庞秀贤，与薛宏亮（未修炼法轮功）被长期关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭依兰县法院庭审。周研被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年， 处罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周艳波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，周艳波毕业于大连医科大学附属卫校，由国家统一分配到大连开发区医院工作，从事临床护理工作。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年，周艳波开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，没有经过任何法律程序，周艳波被劫持到了马三家劳教所，被劳教两年。遭酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被国保警察抓捕后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被视频非法开庭，周艳波被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。目前，周艳波仍被非法关押在大连姚家看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周永杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省农安县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，家住长春市农安县，常在长春市打工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，周永杰被长春市朝阳区宽平派出所抓捕。关押在长春市第四看守所。此后家属未得到任何信息。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年底，周永杰被关押在长春市女子监狱后，家属才得知，她被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周永林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁锦州凌海市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，孙继萍与丈夫周永林被中共绑架、关押，劳教，在派出所、看守所、劳教所遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，孙继萍与丈夫周永林在盘锦市锦采新区大集上告诉人们“法轮大法好”时，被凌海市公安局闫家镇派出所警察绑架，被隔离二十一天后（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日），孙继萍被非法关押到锦州市女子看守所，周永林被非法关押到凌海市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，凌海市法院对孙继萍与丈夫周永林每人各判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚金各一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周玉香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东平度市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>岁生，是平度大泽山镇尹家村一位普通的农村妇女。周玉香<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日与外甥女周君、好友展中香一起到平度仁兆赶集，被仁兆派出所警察抓捕并被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午，周玉香被青岛市黄岛区法院在即墨市普东看守所，通过视频非法庭审，律师做了有理有据的无罪辩护，最后，周玉香被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周远志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周远志（笔名华梁兴、曾仁全）<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日生。是一名自由撰稿人、独立中文笔会会员，由于长期撰写、发表关于各类社会问题及揭露官员腐败的文章，在<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被湖北省钟祥市国家安全局以“涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪”抓捕，获释后周远志在家长期被当局监视居住。根据独立中文笔会的网页显示，他以笔名曾仁全发表多篇敏感文章，其中题目包括“农民以特殊方式表达对江泽民的憎恶”及“人民的名义远离普世价值”。周远志被<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被以“织非法聚集罪”刑事拘留。此前，周远志被指组织访民上访而被当局关押，，被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天原本应于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日释放，但未获释放，随后，被确认其在<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日即遭湖北荆门市公安局东宝分局以“织非法聚集罪”刑事拘留。其妻子张中凤说由于他一向身体不好，她非常担心丈夫的情况。现羁押在荆门市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日在荆门掇刀法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日以“组织非法聚集罪判刑期<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，网上寻衅滋事罪<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，诽谤罪<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，决定合并执行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月”，刑期<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。目前关押地址：<a name="_Hlk52057464">湖北省荆门市东宝区牌楼镇荆门看守所，电话<span lang="EN-US">0724-8882273</span>，邮编<span lang="EN-US">448121<o:p></o:p></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52057464;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">周育琴</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52057464;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省惠东县人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信仰、宣传法轮功，周育琴与石雪梅、刘庆强三人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被惠东县政法委、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办及国保等警方非法抓捕，后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被广东省惠州市惠东县法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密宣判。其中，周育琴被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金五万元<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日</b>）；石雪梅被冤判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）；刘庆强被冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元（刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）。三人均不服审判，已向广东省惠州市中级法院提出上诉。</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">目前被关押在惠东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">周再强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南长沙网民。职业货车司机。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月网上发言支持香港反送中的光复香港、时代革命运动被刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，周再强的亲友才在微信发出消息称：长沙公民周再强近期因在推特上发言支持香港反送中运动而被当局突然抓捕，并以寻衅滋事的罪名刑事拘留，目前已经确认被关押于长沙市第一看守所。据了解，周再强有两个匿名推特号，已持续发推三万多条。香港反送中运动爆发后，他一直都非常关注，也自发和转发了很多推文表示关注和支持。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱凤兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，河南省新乡市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午，在新乡市南高村一出租屋内被河南省新乡市公安局国保警察抓捕。被抢走电脑、打印机等大量个人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，朱凤兰被辉县市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚款一万元。朱凤兰向新乡市中级法院提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，新乡市中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，朱凤兰被关押到新乡市第五女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱凤英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员：石香云、贾艳玲、包义、魏续旺、孔庆艳、朱凤英、赵熙茹、刘君、任秀英、杨骐骥、吴樨、张树霞、宫文义。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被松北区检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被哈尔滨市松北区被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱桂贞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">山东泰安市法轮功信徒，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁的老太太，原泰安市木器厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日下午，朱桂贞和平秀英为了让民众了解法轮大法，在邱家店镇某村，发送法轮功资料，并向路人讲述法轮功受迫害的真相，遭邱家店派出所警察绑架，被关到泰安市看守所。后于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，朱桂贞因修炼法轮功，向百姓传播法轮大法，被泰安市泰山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱海燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏银川市永宁县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年生。大学本科毕业，原宁夏银川市永宁县环境监测中心工作人员，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年底开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，朱海燕多次被抓捕、被关押、劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，朱海燕等<span lang="EN-US">14</span>名法轮功学员被银川市永宁县公安局恶警抓捕、抄家，朱海燕被关押在银川市看守所，后被银川市永宁县公安局构陷到银川市西夏区检察院；遭银川市永宁县公安局和银川市西夏区检察院相互勾结迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被银川市西夏区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱惠来：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">广东省湛江市人，广东省湛江市东海岛东山镇调青北园村村民，抗强拆维权者，民间誉名“东海岛英雄”，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年以来，广东省湛江市政府以“湛江钢铁基地”为名，在无任何批文的前提下（注：该批文直至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才拿到，总值人民币<span lang="EN-US">700</span>亿），烂用公权，派出大批警力对该区域东海岛东简镇衔头村、迈奴村、蓄昌村等八条村以及东山镇北园村等一万多名村民进行暴力拆迁，致使万民怨声载道；因之前朱惠来父子一家不愿意为强拆签字，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，湛江市开发区官员随带领数十人，在没有支付拆迁款的情况下，强毁其田地和家园里的果树、帐棚和农作物等；其子朱培忍开车回来，看到父亲被警方殴打，随前往和其一起与警方、强拆官员发生激烈对抗，最终导致<span lang="EN-US">1</span>死多伤（其中致当地治安大队副队长死亡）；随后，其立即被警方刑拘和逮捕，但却被民间誉为“东海岛英雄”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被广东省湛江市赤坎区中级法院以“故意杀人罪”、“故意伤害罪”一审判处死刑；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，经湛江市赤坎区中级法院二审，改判死缓；其不服，继续上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，广东省高级法院对其案以“事实不清、证据不足”为由“撤销原判、发还重审”；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东省湛江市中级法院再次重审朱惠来父子抗强拆杀官员案，仍判死刑。　<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，广东高院（<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>）粤刑终<span lang="EN-US">298</span>号判决书作出终审判决：朱惠来犯故意杀人罪、故意伤害罪，决定执行死刑，缓期二年执行，剥夺政治权利终身，并限制减刑。目前被羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱家彩：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵州毕节威宁县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十多岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因发放法轮功资料挂横幅，朱家彩、罗翠琴遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在毕节七星关区法院被庭审，后得知朱家彩被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款二万元、罗翠琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，勒索罚款一万元。朱家彩刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">朱建华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">北京朝阳区法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，家住工体附近，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被抓捕，一直被关在昌平东城看守所。后获悉，他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日左右被转到深圳的监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/28/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437388.html#22127221922-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/28/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437388.html#22127221922-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">朱培忍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省湛江市人，广东湛江东海岛东山镇调青北园村村民，“东海岛英雄”，抗暴维权者。自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年以来，广东省湛江市政府以“湛江钢铁基地”为名，在无任何批文的前提下（注：该批文直至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日才拿到，总值人民币<span lang="EN-US">700</span>亿），烂用公权，派出大批警力对该区域东海岛东简镇衔头村、迈奴村、蓄昌村等八条村以及东山镇北园村等一万多名村民进行暴力拆迁，致使万民怨声载道；因之前朱培忍和其父一家不愿意为强拆签字，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，湛江市开发区官员随带领数十人，在没有支付拆迁款的情况下，强毁其父田地和家园里的果树、帐棚和农作物等，其父被严重殴打；其开车回来，看到父亲被警方殴打，随上前与父亲一起与警方、强拆官员发生激烈对抗，最终导致<span lang="EN-US">1</span>死多伤，其随被警方拘捕，但被民间誉为“东海岛英雄”。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被广东省湛江市赤坎区中级法院以“故意杀人罪”、“故意伤害罪”一审判处死缓。其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月经湛江市赤坎区中级法院二审，改判为无期徒刑。其依然不服，继续上诉，至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，广东省高级法院对其案以“事实不清、证据不足”为由“撤销原判、发还重审”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日湛江市中级法院再审朱惠来父子抗暴杀官案，仍为无期徒刑。目前被关押地点不详。其在看守所惨遭酷刑，肝部被打裂，生殖器被打烂，牙齿被打掉，为此曾被送医院抢救。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱素荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，家住河北保定蠡县鲍墟乡东孟尝村，在中孟尝小学任教。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，正在学校上课的朱素荣，突然被鲍墟乡派出所警察骚扰，他们并尾随至家中抄家捕人，当天朱素荣就被送至保定看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月二<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被高阳法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月、勒索罚金五万元，朱素荣已上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">朱孝清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省嫩江市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，家住黑龙江省嫩江市<span lang="EN-US">7</span>星泡农场。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年修炼法轮功。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共集团迫害法轮功后，朱孝清坚持信仰，遭到中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，朱孝清因发放法轮功法轮功资料，被警方抓捕。后被监视居住半年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，朱孝清被当地中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/12/%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9C%B1%E5%AD%9D%E6%B8%85%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-441202.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/12/%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9C%B1%E5%AD%9D%E6%B8%85%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-441202.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱玉芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，江西省萍乡市人，曾为私营企业主，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年因所经营的店铺被时任萍乡市副市长唐湘萍及其丈夫房管局局长家族开办的房地产公司强拆，而走上维权之路。萍乡地方政府在腐败势力操纵下，将朱玉芳作为重点维稳控制和打击对象。在维权过程中，朱玉芳多次被绑架、关黑监狱、遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，因在北京上访维权而被非法拘禁于北京市大兴区某黑监狱<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天，并被与两个男看守放在一个房间，险遭人身侵犯；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，因再次在北京上访而被警方抓捕，并被处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，后又被送至北京市久敬庄非法拘禁<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天，而后被遣返原籍；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾被地方当局长期非法软禁家中，房门被反锁，不准出门；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，因到北京上访而被北京市公安局朝阳警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后因其怀孕又于同日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因其身穿访民反腐文化衫到联合国驻京开发署呼吁要求人权，而被北京市朝阳区警方再次刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因持续在北京上访维权，并将自己遭受迫害经历发于网上，再度被北京警方以“查获访民身份”为由抓走和交由萍乡驻京办事处将其遣返原籍，于遣返当日被萍乡市安源区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，并关押于萍乡市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被江西省萍乡市安源区法院一审以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，经江西省萍乡市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，后送江西省女子监狱服刑；出狱后，其一直就被枉法冤判申诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，因又到到江西省高级法院申诉，遭拒，随就在法院门外举牌呼吁；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日（即世界人权日），其突遭失联，后知被江西省萍乡市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，不到一周即被萍乡市安源区检察院批准逮捕，羁押在萍乡市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_22.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_22.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱宇飙：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月出生，广东省人，原广州地铁小额贷款有限公司职员，原广东金粤律师事务所、广州市广大律师事务所、广东恒益律师事务所执业律师，广东省第一个公开为法轮功信仰者作无罪辩护的正义律师，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。学生时代，曾就读于广东省中山大学法学专业；法学硕士毕业后，先后曾就职于广东金粤律师事务所、广州市广大律师事务所和广东恒益律师事务所，作执业律师；因为经常热心为弱势群体当事人作代理辩护律师，并以低价或折价收费，甚至不计报酬，所以深受社会大众及业界同仁称许、好评；但因其练习和信仰法轮功而屡遭政府打压逼迫，遂被迫多次转换律所，直至最终其律师执业证被广东司法当局吊销；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，曾分别为三名法轮功信仰者做无罪辩护，因其法庭辩护词精彩绝伦，堪称经典，顿令中共法庭大为震惊和难堪，随后即被广东司法当局称为“反革命”，将其列为广东省公安厅要维稳严控的“头号人物”；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其突然被广州市警方野蛮抓捕，后被枉法处劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，送广州市第三劳教所关押；关押期间，曾遭多次酷刑折磨，如“坐老虎凳”、“架飞机”、用湿毛巾盖脸窒息、水淹、在冷天灌凉水、鞭打手指及脚趾、不准睡觉，等等；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，劳教释放后，因其律师证被广州当局故意拖延办理，对其工作和日常生活造成极大不便；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其第二次被广州市海珠区新港派出所警方莫名抓捕、刑拘，家遭查抄，后被广州市海珠区法院以“利用邪教破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并送广东省北江监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，虽是其刑满获释日，但又被转送到广东省三水洗脑班非法关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，再次被广州市海珠区警方十余人闯入抄家，搜走几本其个人阅读的法轮功书籍之后，随即将其绑架到一不知名的法轮功洗脑班关押；据悉，自其被抓至今，家人一直无法知其更多信息。目前被羁押地点不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱兆水：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省舒兰市吉舒镇法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。一九九八年开始修炼法轮功。曾被非法劳教一年多。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚被当地警方抓捕、关押；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月中旬获悉，朱兆水被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">朱作亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，浙江省金华市金东区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，朱作亮曾被中共抓捕，关押，并分别在南宁市看守所、杭州市看守所、十里坪劳教所及监狱遭多种酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾被“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”头目曹秋水等抓捕到金华双龙洗脑班迫害，之后又被劫持到金华市看守所，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，朱作亮被劫入浙江省第四监狱继续迫害<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月以后，在中共邪党的“清零”迫害中，被要求签“三书”（即诬陷法轮功，并签放弃法轮功的保证），被其当面拒绝，随因坚持信仰被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被庭审。据悉，朱作亮被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现被关押在金华看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/1/%E6%9B%BE%E9%99%B7%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E5%85%AD%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E6%B5%99%E6%B1%9F%E6%9C%B1%E4%BD%9C%E4%BA%AE%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%98%E5%AF%86%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430300.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/1/%E6%9B%BE%E9%99%B7%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1%E5%85%AD%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E6%B5%99%E6%B1%9F%E6%9C%B1%E4%BD%9C%E4%BA%AE%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%98%E5%AF%86%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430300.html</span></a></span><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">祝亚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉市黄陂区法轮功学员，祝亚是个残疾人，家住武汉市黄陂区前川街，丈夫早逝，她与女儿相依为命。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，祝亚去买菜，被便衣警察拦截。这次抓捕祝亚是由省城“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”亲自操控、指使的，他们闯进家中抄家。武汉市黄陂区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日庭审，被秘密枉判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">珠扎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">现年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县求吉玛乡索日玛村人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。因政治诉求，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年曾被当局以不详政治罪名抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被警方以涉嫌“组织阿坝民众举办达赖喇嘛<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁寿辰活动”为罪由，从其僧舍强行带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其已被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 119.25pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">珠玛别克<span lang="EN-US">.</span>穆汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">42</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，新疆阿尔泰市人，阿尔泰市喀拉希力克乡武装部官员，哈萨克族政治犯。曾因被新疆中共当局指控在聊天工具微信“乱说话”，“泄漏中共党内机密”，而于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被阿尔泰市警方刑拘、逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，获悉近期已被新疆阿尔泰市法院以“泄露国家机密罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。据称，其原本在上海读大学的儿子因父亲被判刑，竟遭株连，被校方勒令退学，现已回到新疆家中。其妻子古丽加丽拉也因受牵连，原本在乡政府卫生院工作，也因此被辞退，他本人在银行的<span lang="EN-US">60</span>万元人民币积蓄遭罚没，家里的<span lang="EN-US">50</span>头牛也被政府没收。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">庄友布：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">42</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，福建省宁德市福鼎县人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨贵媚、杨雄、陈开奇，林丽芳、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，庄友布被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中，庄友布被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邹华兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，今年<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生，重庆长寿区法轮功学员，原重庆长寿农机公司退休职工，邹华兰因修炼法轮功曾多次遭受迫害：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次劳教，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次判刑，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被关洗脑班，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次关押在看守所将近<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，中共政法委书记郭声琨到重庆开会，要求对跨区域活动的维权人士、法轮功学员等要重点打击。重庆市长寿区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>和国保为了完成所谓的“政治任务”，也为了捞取升官资本，开始寻找他们的下手目标。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，邹华兰在贵州结束冤狱回家。因为这段被外省判刑的经历，邹华兰成了长寿区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>和国保的迫害对象。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右，长寿区国保支队指使晏家街道派出所警察，到贵州去调查邹华兰被构陷的案子，作为再次迫害的“证据”。然后，又以监控摄像头摄到邹华兰在晏家街道发台历为借口，晏家派出所几个警察，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">33</span>日，闯入邹华兰家中，把邹华兰抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，邹华兰被逮捕，后被关押在长寿区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，邹华兰被重庆市江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邹佩霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东东营法轮功学员。耿录堂、邹佩霞老夫妻，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年已年过七旬，家住东营市胜利油田孤岛采油厂芙蓉小区。修炼大法前，夫妻俩身体很不好，耿录堂还患有高血压等疾病。一九九六年前后，老俩口修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，老俩口去河口地区赶集，向人宣传法轮功，遭人恶告，东营市河口区国保大队下属的义和镇派出所警察，于当天抓捕了夫妇俩。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开庭，后耿录堂、邹佩霞夫妇均被东营市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并被勒索罚款三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邹幸彤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，英语名：<span lang="EN-US">Tonyee Chow Hang-tung</span>，原英属香港籍人，现中华人民共和国（香港）公民，香港大律师，原香港支联会副主席，第<span lang="EN-US">35</span>届“中国杰出民主人士奖”荣获者，民主人权斗士，社会活动家，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于英国剑桥大学哈默顿学院物理学系，毕业后又在香港大学专业进修学院研读法律专业，而后成为一名香港执业大律师；自<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年起，因致力于中国的民主人权事业， 随开始担任香港支联会（即香港市民支持爱国民主运动联合会）副主席，期间，曾积极推动和举办了每年的维多利亚公园（简称“维园”）<span lang="EN-US">64</span>纪念烛光晚会；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，当李卓人、何俊仁等香港民主前辈和支联会高层相继 遭遇中共香港政府的迫害身陷囹圄时，其勇敢的站出来，成为继续组织香港市民纪念<span lang="EN-US">64</span>活动的主要领导者；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，在中共主导下的港版“国安法”管控下，支联会被香港警方以防疫（<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>冠状病毒疾病，<span lang="EN-US">COVID-19</span>）为由禁止在维园举行当晚的悼念<span lang="EN-US">64 </span>烛光晚会；针此，支联会立即提起上诉，但因上诉很快被驳回，故其公开表态自己会以个人名义到场纪念；次日，即被警方以涉嫌“宣传未经批准集结”为由拘捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，暂获取保候审，但<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，又因拒绝在限期内向香港国安处提交支联会的文件而再被港警拘捕；次日，又被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”和支联会主席李卓人、副主席何俊仁等共计<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人一起正式起诉，被指控因在社交网络和媒体发表意在鼓动民众参与未经批准的六四集会言论，其等言行已触犯港版《国安法》的相关法令，故应予量刑；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其一行<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人案被香港法院统一宣判，其中，其被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”和<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年“煽动他人参与纪念<span lang="EN-US">64</span>集会罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年（<span lang="EN-US">12</span>个月）；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又被香港法院以<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年两次 “煽动他人参与纪念六四集会罪” 判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月（<span lang="EN-US">15</span>个月）；因先后两次判决的一部分刑期同时执行，故其最后实际执行刑期<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月（<span lang="EN-US">22</span>个月 ）；据悉，庭审中其拒绝认罪，坚称其发帖与撰文旨在呼吁人们勿忘六四，并非鼓动众人聚集闹事。目前在香港监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_69.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_69.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">左洪涛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局在左洪涛、崔秋荣夫妇开的“佳合中介”抓捕了夫妻二人及吴文章、杨晓勇、袁素静及李国爱等五名法轮功学员，抄查中野蛮地抢劫了中介周转资金十余万元现金及电动车一辆和其它办公用品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，山海关区检察院侦监科科长陈铁忠对左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。左洪涛刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">结束语：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告是一份月度动态报告，这是第<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">79</span></b>期，肯定仍然会有遗漏和信息滞后的情况。希望大陆各地的人权捍卫者积极补充，请将符合本报告标准而未统计人员情况、以及本报告名单人员的最新情况提供给我们，以便使以后的报告更加翔实和完善。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">维权网联系方法：<span lang="EN-US">wqw2011@gmail.com</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2022</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">附录：本月获悉上期名录中刑满释放<span lang="EN-US">27</span>人、死亡<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人，共计<span lang="EN-US">28</span>的名单<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刑满释放<span lang="EN-US">27</span>人：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">阿旺益西（藏）、边巴杰布（藏）、陈家鸿、陈鹰军、程全云、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">董维兴、董玉英、范志刚、郭延达、何秀兰、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">姜海英、李赛美、李晓波、秦莲玉、曲嘉唯色（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王艺霖、王尊建、谢红英、许秀芬、姚旺、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">应国芳、于春香、张桂芝、张华、仲周（藏）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贡却才培（藏）、陈文胜<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">死亡<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丹增曲卡（藏）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">共计：<span lang="EN-US">28</span>人<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、阿旺益西：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">藏族，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年代出生，西藏自治区拉萨市林周县人，拉萨市林周县旁多乡村民，生态环境保护者，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。自</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1998</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年始，中共西藏当局即在西藏拉萨所辖的林周县旁多乡境内对各种矿产资源进行初步勘探，并为防止当地藏人进行抗议，曾特意宣布将为无业藏人提供工作机会等，但在正式开工采矿，且顺利修建“旁多水利枢纽工程”之后，当局不仅不兑现之前的承诺，反而随意开采矿区，使得当地生态环境遭受严重破坏（如）；迫于无耐，当地藏人遂多次向相关部门提出反映与投诉；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2009</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月，西藏当局为确保水利工程及采矿等计划顺利实行，开始强令旁多乡</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">119</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">户（近</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">700</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名）村民集体搬迁；因当地藏民拒不搬迁，虽数次向主管部门提出投诉请求，均毫无果效，随于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2011</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被迫开展和平示威活动，试图阻拦破坏生态环境的采矿项目，但又遭到中共军警的残酷镇压；很快，阿旺益西与另</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名村民维权代表均被拉萨市警方野蛮抓捕，自此失联；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2012</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，在被超期拘押长达</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年多之久后，其一行</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">人“请愿游行案”在拉萨市中级法院开庭受理，均被以“试图分裂西藏，并组织领导了以保护环境为名的抗议活动”罪由分别重判</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8-12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年不等刑期，其中，阿旺益西被秘密判处有期徒刑</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，判决书刑期至</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月。在西藏自治区第一监狱（原拉萨市扎其监狱）服刑。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、边巴杰布</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：藏族，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年代出生，又称边巴坚参，西藏自治区拉萨市林周县人，拉萨市林周县旁多乡村民，职业不详，生态环境保护者，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。自</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1998</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年始，中共西藏当局即在西藏拉萨所辖的林周县旁多乡境内对各种矿产资源进行初步勘探，并为防止当地藏人进行抗议，曾特意宣布将为无业藏人提供工作机会等，但在正式开工采矿，且顺利修建“旁多水利枢纽工程”之后，当局不仅不兑现之前的承诺，反而随意开采矿区，使得当地生态环境遭受严重破坏；迫于无耐，当地藏人遂多次向相关部门提出反映与投诉，但毫无效果； </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2009</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月，西藏当局为确保水利工程及采矿等计划如期举行，开始强令旁多乡</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">119</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">户（近</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">700</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名）村民集体搬迁；后因当地藏民拒绝搬迁，数次向主管部门提出长久居住要求，均无果效，随于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2011</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月，被迫开展和平抗议活动，以期借此拦阻当局破坏生态环境的采矿项目，但又遭到中共军警的残酷镇压； 很快，边巴杰布及另</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名维权村民代表被拉萨市警方野蛮抓捕，自此失联；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2012</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，边巴杰布家属获悉，在被秘押长达一年多之久后，其一行</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">6</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">人“请愿游行案”在拉萨市中级法院开庭受理，均被以“试图分裂西藏，并组织领导了以保护环境为名的抗议活动”罪由重判</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8-12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年不等刑期，其中，边巴杰布与另两名维权藏人（曲嘉唯色、阿旺益西）分别被秘密判处有期徒刑</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，判决书刑期至</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月。曾在西藏自治区第一监狱（原拉萨市扎其监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、陈家鸿</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：又名陈文胆，字数真。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生于北流隆盛镇平坡村立新组。<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年容县师范毕业后在北流从教，后获北京科技进修学院律师函授班结业，中国逻辑与语言函授大学行政法专业毕业。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年分别在北流市、玉林市创办了老好人写作代理和金头脑文案写作代理服务部。后陈家鸿通过司法考试在广西百举鸣律师事务所执业，成为一名正式执业律师。源于陈家鸿长期参与维权敏感案件从而不断遭到当局的打压。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月底，陈家鸿律师介入了震惊网络的“广西村民罗继标在看守所离奇死亡事件”，曾遭广西警持枪围困。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，广西律协官网发布了对陈家鸿律师的“公开谴责行业处分的通报”。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份，陈家鸿律师被南宁市司法局行政处罚停业半年。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，广西南宁市司法局宣布解散百举鸣律师事务所，所有律师被要求转去其他律所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，陈家鸿律师被北流市公安局、玉林市公安局联合抓捕，家中也被抄了一些卷宗和其他东西。后获知被刑事拘留。后遭批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，陈家鸿涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权案”在广西玉林市中级人民法院开审。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">其一直坚称无罪，且因患有高血压及脑萎缩等病症，健康状况极差。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，玉林市中院宣判陈家鸿煽动颠覆国家政权罪成，判处有期徒刑三年。目前被羁押于广西玉林市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_81.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_81.html</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、陈鹰军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西咸阳网民陈鹰军、王兴杰等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>人因在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群传播涉及政治的内容于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被咸阳市秦都区法院以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半有期徒刑。判决书指控他们通过<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群有组织地传播“涉及政治的谣言”，攻击政府、党和国家领导人。被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名陕西咸阳网民分别是：陈鹰军、王兴杰、卢向辉、刘芗、周昱、朱远亮、李好轩、徐海波、李泰营、周福评、潘建、廖焕华、武刚。其中，<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">陈鹰军在庭审中只高喊口号，不做辩护，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期最重。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、程全云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京通州法轮功学员。程全云<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被抓捕抄家，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被批捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源<span lang="EN-US">:<o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan;
