font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、董维兴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省四平市伊通县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，四平市伊通县教师进修学校教师。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，董维兴被伊通县公安局国保警察抓捕，被关押在伊通县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，董维兴被伊通县法院庭审；四月初获悉，董维兴被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、董玉英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安市鄠邑区法轮功女学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月出生。鄠邑区两名法轮功女学员王红、董玉英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在鄠邑区将村镇附近讲真相时，被人恶意举报，被将村镇派出所警察抓捕，关押在西安市莲湖区看守所。被西安市莲湖区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元，枉判刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日止。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/27/2021-8-27.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/27/2021-8-27.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">8</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、范志刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省葫芦岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，范志刚和妻子苏爽被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被葫芦岛市山区法院庭审，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日法院下达的判决书，范志刚被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；苏爽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、郭延达：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省营口市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年六十一岁。被抓捕迫害前，在市内某大酒店当过厨师，因修炼法轮功，郭延达<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被营口市站前区东桥派出所警察从家中抓捕。警察抄走郭延达家的私有财产：电脑、打印机、钱、汽车及一些物品。现在被关押在辽宁省沈阳市第一监狱第二监区。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日辽宁省营口市站前区法院对营口市法轮功学员郭延达等庭审，后得知郭延达被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> </b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、何秀兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，英文名：<span lang="EN-US">Cyd Ho Sau-lan</span>，原英属香港籍人，现中华人民共和国（香港）籍中西区薄扶林公民，绰号“何姨姨”、“何<span lang="EN-US">EE</span>”，香港<span lang="EN-US">LGBT</span>权利运动（又称同志权利运动）、性工作者及妇女权利运动维护者，前香港电台及多个网络电台节目主持人，前独立民间团体香港人权监察主席，前线（本土政党组织）首任召集人，工党创党副主席，前香港立法会议员，前香港中西区区议员，原公民起动（本土政党组织）成立人和召集人，泛民主派会议召集人，中国在押政治犯。自幼生长于英属香港；<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年从香港中五毕业后，又在香港浸会学院（今香港浸会大学）攻读英国文学系；<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-1979</span>年，曾在加拿大安大略省的滑铁卢大学继续修读，但未能毕业；后返回香港，曾于<span lang="EN-US">1979</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-1995</span>年从事成衣制造出口业；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年－<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年－<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，曾担任香港立法会议员，并担任泛民会议召集人数年；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年－<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年，曾又当选为香港中西区（观龙选区）区议员；历任议员期间，曾就《最低工资条例草案》联同李卓人等泛民主派议员向立法会提出<span lang="EN-US">11</span>项修订，如最低工资委员会组成方法及职能、立法会是否有权提出工资水平的修订动议等；曾提出多项与民生有关的建议，如劳工最低工资设限及标准工时立法等）；曾要求立法会召开特别会议，讨论警方在反预算案游行中涉嫌使用过分武力驱散集会者（如未预先警告便动用胡椒喷雾，以及有警察插眼、拳打示威者）的投诉；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2013</span>年，曾就多项有关香港民权（如《教育条例》修订）和小众平权（如“同志平权”、《性倾向歧视条例》落实等）问题提出议案或动议；曾提出动议，要求港府引用特权法成立专责委员会调查前香港廉政专员、保安局署理常任秘书长、海关关长及第<span lang="EN-US">12</span>届全国政协委员汤显明涉贪问题，但以上议案或动议均遭建制派在分组点票下否决；同期，曾就修订<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年香港行政长官民主普选程序提出议案，要求准许参选人只要获<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万名选民联署，即可成为行政长官候选人；曾提倡泛民各政党以“欧盟模式”结盟合作，集中力量与资源推举有执政能力的候选人参加特首选举，以应对未来普选的挑战；曾约见独立监察警方处理投诉委员会并与对方会面，要求关注警方在执法时能否维持政治中立；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，因泛民委员不满建制派袒护立法会调查前廉政专员汤显明的涉贪问题，拒绝为其签名承认报告，随其曾严厉批评建制派处事不公，对泛民调查工作设卡，明显“阻止有志反贪的议员调查下去”；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2016</span>年，其在成为泛民主派会议召集人之后，曾积极提出私人草案把特首纳入《防止贿赂条例》规管范围，要求设立<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人独立委员会，负责批核特首收受的利益，修补现行机制漏洞；曾就版权条例修订草案提岀修正案，要求香港效法加拿大采用开放式豁免，即全面豁免非牟利个人用途的作品，但被港府以全球只有加拿大有先例为由反对；曾在立法会审议《<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年拨款条例草案》时，连同多名民主派议员提出批评性意见，要求削减平等机会委员会主席陈章明的<span lang="EN-US">28 0</span>万元年薪，指陈在立法保障性小众免受歧视方面欠缺承担和认知；曾在全国人大委员长张德江访港时拒绝出席欢庆酒会，并拟在会面期间向其递交泛民联署声明，要求重启香港政改和更换特首，后其在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年的香港立法会选举中终致败选，自此结束立法会议员生涯。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">15</span>名民主派人士突遭香港警方拘捕，被控其等因参加<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月期间三次未经批准的集会和游行，故而违反了港版《国安法》之规条；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其案在香港西九龙裁判法院开始庭审，但因该案件分三案处理，需暂停再审，随以交<span lang="EN-US">1,000</span>元保释；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其一行多人案再次庭审，其虽承认是被告之一，但拒绝认罪，至同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，仍被西九龙法院以“组织未经批准集结罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前服刑监狱缺详。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_45.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_45.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">11</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、姜海英</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：山东省高密市拒城河社区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，高密市密水街道拒成河社区法轮功学员姜海英在外讲法轮功被迫害的真相，被李家营派出所抓捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，已押到济南女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">12</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、李赛美：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖南长沙市开福区法轮功学员。李赛美于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚十一点左右被一帮长沙警察抄家并抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉，李赛美被判刑一年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。 <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/28/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-435417.html#211227211729-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/28/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-435417.html#211227211729-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">13</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、李晓波：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省人，前四川省仁寿县副书记、前四川省蒲江县县长，原某房产公司总经理，法轮功修炼者，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年中共将法轮功定为“邪教”之后，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年遂被四川省成都市警方逮捕，并被当地法院以“邪教罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，关押于四川省德阳监狱，受尽摧残折磨，直至<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年才准予获释；出狱后，其信仰意志弥坚，继续进行法轮功修炼并传播法轮功真相，遂遭致当局的严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，因其在成都市龙泉驿区金堂县给村民散发法轮功真相传单，被当地洪安派出所警方强行抓走（注：当时被野蛮抓捕的还有其子李喆，后因李喆已是加拿大籍公民，遂被当局强行遣回加拿大）并被刑拘，其家被抄，且所有被抄物品包括四台计算机和打印机等，均不给开据任何没收清单；后被正式逮捕，超期关押于四川省成都市龙泉驿看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，终被四川省成都市龙泉驿法院再次以“利用邪教组织颠覆国家法律罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。目前在四川省德阳监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">14</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、秦莲玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江宁波市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，宁波市二十多名法轮功学员被当局绑架，遭受不同程度的迫害，秦莲玉被关押在宁波市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，在宁波市镇海区法院，秦莲玉案第二次被开庭，其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款六千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">15</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、曲嘉唯色（藏）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">西藏拉萨市林周县人，林周县旁多村村民，生态环境保护者，村民维权代表，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年以来，中共当局以资源开发为由，一直在西藏拉萨市林周县旁多乡进行“旁多水利枢纽工程”建设，为防止反对声音，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年两次召集当地藏民开会，强调该工程因是中共高层指令，若有藏人反对，就将以政治罪名论处；然而，随着相关部门施工工作的运作，不仅在当地进行长时间的测量、建桥及建路等，还接连不断的在旁多村和宁布村一带炸山挖石，肆意开采矿产，导致当地生态环境严重受损，同时附近民房出现裂痕、大面积农田被毁坏；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，该水利枢纽工程正式开工，当局宣称自同<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日起试运行后，该工程“将对增强城市防洪和改善城乡供水能力、改善生态环境等发挥巨大的作用”，但此一举却引来其家乡村民的十分不满，并称当局是以建设水利工程为名，行掠夺资源之实；与此同时，曾因当局多次强迫其家乡旁多村<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多户（近<span lang="EN-US">700</span>人）藏民整村搬迁，随引起藏民的集体反对；其作为村民维权代表，曲嘉唯色与他人多次前往当地管理部门投诉请愿，但无任何效果，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被迫再次发起请愿游行，以期借此阻拦破坏生态环境的采矿项目，但却遭到中共军警的残酷镇压，包括其在内的<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名村民维权代表被拉萨市警方野蛮抓捕，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，曲嘉唯色等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人请愿游行案在拉萨市中级法院开庭受理，均被以“试图分裂西藏，并组织领导了以保护环境为名的抗议活动”罪由分别重判<span lang="EN-US">8-12</span>年不等刑期，曲嘉唯色亦被秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，判决书刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。曾在西藏自治区第一监狱（原拉萨市扎其监狱）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">16</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、王艺霖 ：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，吉林长春市法轮功学员。王艺霖于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在南湖公园讲法轮功法轮功，被南湖派出所警察关押，关押于苇子沟行政拘留所<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后，又被抓捕到长春市第<span lang="EN-US">4</span>看守所，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被长春市公安局朝阳分局刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被朝阳分局以所谓的“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”逮捕。被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日左右被第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次庭审，据悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">17</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、王尊建：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北籍公民。<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生，因言获罪于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被刑事拘留，羁押在云梦县第一看守所，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被执行逮捕，被控罪名为涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”。据湖北省孝感市中级法院在二审裁定书：当局指控王尊建于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月间，多次到敏感案件、事件的现场围观、声援；在网络上炒作、声援敏感案件、事件和特定人物，辱骂、诋毁党和国家领导人，利用网络平台破坏社会管理秩序，情节恶劣，构成寻衅滋事罪。其中包括<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>号在武汉市青山公安分局门口参与声援秦永敏涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪一案；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日转发镇江老兵维权事件；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月转发、发布大量香港社会反送中运动的相关信息；发布纪念六四三十周年的相关言论；等等。因此，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日云梦县法院一审判决王尊建有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王尊建上诉后，二审维持了原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">18</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、谢红英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">甘肃省酒泉市肃州区法轮功学员。谢红英于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被抓捕，当日被抄家抓捕关押。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉，谢红英于被判刑一年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/28/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-435417.html#211227211729-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">19</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、许秀芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京房山区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共江泽民集团开始迫害法轮功后，许秀芬坚定大法修炼，因此多次被抓捕、关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，许秀芬被拘留十<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月十<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，又被拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，许秀芬被劳教两年半，在内蒙古图牧吉劳教所受到酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日再次被抓捕、构陷，后被房山法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。妹妹许秀红遭酷刑、药物等迫害，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日含冤离世，年仅<span lang="EN-US">40</span>岁。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、姚旺：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午案受害人。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2020</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：姚旺被判</span>有有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">21</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、应国芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江省宁波市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，应国芳被宁波警察抓捕抄家。后获悉应国芳被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被关押在宁波市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被关押到浙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">22</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、于春香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。于春香是一位温柔贤惠的妻子，是一个孝顺善良的女儿、儿媳妇，是一个负责的母亲，是一个慷慨、处处为他人着想的好邻居，是一个爱帮助别人而不计回报的人，是一个从不贪图便宜，甚至宁愿自己吃亏、也看不得别人吃亏的善良人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，于春香遭便衣人恶告，被大连站北广场派出所、西岗分局警察绑架抄家，被关押到拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，大连市西岗区法院在没通知家属、也没有律师到场的情况下，突然非法对于春香所谓“开庭”审理。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，于春香被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">23</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、张桂芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市通河县法轮功学员，哈尔滨医科大学本科毕业，本是通河县妇幼保健院主治医师，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早，公安局一张桂芝和另一位法轮功学员被绑架。后张桂芝被判刑五年，在黑龙江省女子监狱遭受迫害，曾经被关小号，戴脚镣。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，张桂芝在通河县邮政局邮寄劝善信，邮局工作人员拒邮后，说要请示一下领导。接着“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”国保大队五人，抓捕了张桂芝。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，哈尔滨市依兰县第三法院对张桂芝庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获知，张桂芝被哈尔滨市依兰县第三法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">24</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、张华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福州市鼓楼区五凤街道居民，因家里店铺被强拆而走上维权道路，为人善良，经常帮助其他维权公民。因上访维权，张华长期被户籍所在地政府作为维稳对象。据信，这次张华在北京被绑架、强迫失踪，与北京即将在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初召开全国“两会”有关。每当“人大代表”在北京开会的时候，需要这些“人民代表”解决问题的人民，就要被清理出北京。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日凌晨，张华在北京市丰台区王佐镇的租住处，被不明身份人员撬开房门抓走，当日被带回福州市，关押在速<span lang="EN-US">8</span>酒店<span lang="EN-US">8605</span>房间（福州西环北路店，福州市鼓楼区梦山路<span lang="EN-US">198</span>号），期间遭到殴打。张华通过手机发出上述消息后，其手机处于关机状态，外界无法再联系到张华本人。怀疑其手机已被夺走。福州西环北路速<span lang="EN-US">8</span>酒店属于福州鼓西路派出所管辖，张华家属向派出所报警，不被受理。负责维稳张华的，是福州市鼓楼区五凤街道办事处党工委副书记郑亮，其电话<span lang="EN-US">13509351160</span>。后于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被放回家。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_23.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_23.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_71.html<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">25</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、仲周（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州人，又叫“尊珠”，阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其协助侄子兼徒弟、同寺僧人彭措（又叫平措，已于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日自焚死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁）为纪念中共当局镇压拉萨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件三周年，抗议中共政府对藏人的强权高压统治，以自焚方式（指一种藏人抗议暴政、伸张正义的方式，即藏人自焚者把自己整个奉献出来，以清晰的理智、自愿的心态和惨烈的方式向暴政表达最强烈抗议的无奈选择，以期使公众舆论对极权和高压统治者予以最强烈的谴责或改变对手的情感）在阿坝县城洽唐中街实施自焚行动；同时，因其担心当局野蛮抢夺自焚尸体，而将自焚后的彭措转移隐藏到格尔登寺内，由此引发中共军警与当地僧人、藏人的激烈对抗和冲突；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其随被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康县警方抓捕，并被以“安排转移、藏匿彭措达<span lang="EN-US">11</span>个小时之久，导致彭措因为体表大面积烧伤、延误救治而死亡”为罪由刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被四川省马尔康县法院以“故意杀人罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。判决书刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">26</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、贡却才培（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Kunchok Tsephel Gopey Tsang</span>，甘肃省甘南藏族自治州玛曲县欧拉乡人，曾担任玛曲县藏文中学英语教师，并任玛曲县畜牧局公务员、藏语及藏族网络作家和琼迈藏语文学网编辑，政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年曾因涉嫌政治活动而被拘押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，后无罪获释；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年因在互联网上发表了与西藏<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件有关的文章，同时向外界披露藏人在抗议事件中被镇压、军警抓捕寺院僧侣等消息，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被从家中逮捕，并遭搜查，之后与外界失去联系；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被甘肃省甘南藏族自治州中级法院秘密审判，以“泄露国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，原刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。因他在监狱里救了另一个正在服刑的藏人，表现良好而于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日提前释放。此前在甘肃省甘南自治州合作监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/15.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/15.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.rfa.org/english/news/tibet/writer-03222022121939.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">https://www.rfa.org/english/news/tibet/writer-03222022121939.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">27</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、陈文胜：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1969</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，湖南省衡阳市石鼓区人，衡阳市石鼓区西湖一村<span lang="EN-US">13</span>栋<span lang="EN-US">507</span>户公民，职业不详，基督徒，湖南衡阳小群教会信徒，街头传道人，中国曾押良心犯。早年曾吸毒成性十余年，后因在戒毒所听到福音而成为基督徒，并凭信心而除掉了毒瘾，故而自此致力于广传基督教福音；曾因经常举着写有“荣耀救主”、“悔改信靠得救”的十字架独自上街宣传，或与教会其他基督徒一起走街串巷，到城市闹市区（甚至到过西藏）传福音，随屡遭当局打压，多次被警方警告、威胁和被关押在衡阳市拘留所，甚至一年之中竟有<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，曾因到广西壮族自治区宣传基督教福音，而被南宁市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又因上街传福音，而被湖南省衡阳市石鼓区警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，因与另一基督教信徒一起先后在衡阳市商业步行街附近和中医医院附近，利用喇叭、广播播放及发福音单张等方式宣传基督教，而被衡阳市蒸湘区警方以“扰乱社会秩序”为由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，因与其母为跨农历新年传福音，而被衡阳市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；之后，因其继续走街串巷传福音，而在该年又曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因到浙江省传福音，而被辖区警方跨境抓捕，后被指定居所监视居住于西湖山庄，<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天后，才在轮番轰炸般的约谈之后予以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因其到云南向少数民族朋友传福音，同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，即被云南省文山壮族苗族自治州文山市警方拦截，且被移交给衡阳市警方遣回原籍；获释后，其接续外出传福音，甚至向国保警方和当地街道办事处工作人员等传福音；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因其到湖南省益阳市安化县传福音，被衡阳市政法委、统战部及国保警方联合跨区抓回，次日被衡阳市青山派出所警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其重获自由，此前曾被羁押于衡阳市拘留所。但释放当天又去上街传福音；据悉，其妻子、儿媳及孙女等家人因受牵连，曾遭当局多次恐吓和威胁，被要求务必说服、阻止其外出传福音，否则不仅儿媳会被单位开除公职，而且其孙女也会在将来不能考取国家公务员与教师等工作。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_0.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_0.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">死亡<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人：丹增曲卡（藏）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、丹增曲卡：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，西藏自治区拉萨市人，又名丹曲，藏名<span lang="EN-US"> Tenzin Choedak</span>或<span lang="EN-US">Tenchoe</span>，社会工作者，中国曾押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代在印度达兰萨拉的西藏儿童村完成<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年级的教育课程；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年返回西藏，在当地的欧洲非政府组织红十字会工作，并在拉萨和日喀则等多个地区推动环保工作；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因参与拉萨的和平抗议活动，被当地警方拘捕；据悉，在拘捕期间曾遭遇严刑逼供，理由是其父曾在西藏政治舞台上活跃多年，但<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年被迫离开西藏流亡印度，严刑拷打他目的是确定其抗议行动是否受到父亲的影响；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被拉萨市中级法院以“间谍罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，并处罚款人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；刑期应至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日；据悉，其在狱中惨遭酷刑折磨，致其吐血、脑部损伤，身体备受摧残；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，其家人得知其被狱方紧急送往医院，称其手、腿在送达医院时已经严重粉碎性骨折；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，其在保外就医第二天，不治身亡。此前在西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱（西藏自治区拉萨市曲水县聂当乡 ，邮编<span lang="EN-US"> 850600</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_42.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_42.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p> <p align="left"
